For unsolicited attachments, the Provider invokes this operation before, concurrently, or after  the claim or pre-authorization transaction. For solicited attachments, the Provider invokes it when responding to a Payer request for attachments or additional information. Any HTTP endpoint can use $submit-attachment, not just FHIR RESTful server endpoints. Implementers of CDex's Unsolicited Attachments SHOULD support the Endpoint Discovery Strategy defined in the Da Vinci HRex specification to allow discovery of the endpoint for this operation. For Solicited Attachments, the $submit-attachment endpoint is supplied in the CDex Task Attachment Request Profile' (BUSINESSRULE)
